Judge Diplomacy Player Ratings


Games In the Database as of January 1, 2003

The games listed here are all either (a) included in Nick Fitzpatrick's Hall of Fame, Issue 21, (b) are included (in summary format) in Nick's group of games that are due to be added to the *next* issue of the HoF, or (c) are recent games that have been emailed (in summary format) to my database -- many from the YARS database at the Diplomatic Pouch.

I'm just showing the game name and judge (which, together, make up a unique identifier (with just a couple of exceptions)). If you played in a game and it isn't on this list, then you definitely did *not* get credit for it in the Archive.

Some games have "Irregular Flags" associated with them, which indicates something different about that game. Some irregular flags (B, C, D, F, H, J, L, N, O, P, V, and Z) mean that the game does not count towards the calculation of player ratings -- either the DRR or the JDPR. The DRR also does *not* use Real-Time Dip games (those with an "X" flag). The description of the irregular flags is taken from Nick's Hall of Fame: 

Irregular Codes
---------------
A NMR--not significant (NMR flag was set)
B NMR--significant (whether NMR flag was set, or not)
C Abandoned game
D Same-Site
E Any-Site (this is no longer being recorded as an irregularity)
F Any-Site, but many players from Same-Site
G Reduced victory condition
H Variant not eligible for HoF points
I Player returned as 2nd power, after being eliminated
J Player returned as 2nd power, without being eliminated
K Player returned as 2nd power, without being eliminated (mercy position)
L Player played two (or more) powers simultaneously
M Player played two (or more) powers simultaneously (mercy position)
N GM played in game he GMed
O Judge-keeper played in game on his judge
P Players appear to have communicated in a gunboat game
Q Computer program played a power
R Increased victory condition
S Player returned to game as GM after being eliminated
T GM imposed win or draw
U Two family members played in same game (no effect on game)
V Two family members played in same game (affected game)
W GM played in game he GMed (mercy position)
X Real-time game
Z Other problem that made game irregular

If you have a game summary that isn't included here or a correction to the irregular flags for a game listed here, please email me, Doug Massey.
